OBX||TX|APRESULT^.|37|  can occur. The test should be performed at regular intervals, and||||||F
OBX||TX|APRESULT^.|38|  positive results should be confirmed before definitive therapy.||||||F
OBX||TX|APRESULT^.|39|  Additional testing methods may be helpful in detecting abnormalities or||||||F
OBX||TX|APRESULT^.|40|  in clinical management.||||||F
